msg:I rarely write reviews. I booked for three days. When I arrived on the first day, I asked the staff who helped me with the suitcase what time the swimming pool would open, but they couldn't answer... It didn't seem very professional. The room was still big, but there were black marks on the wall and the sofa was cracked... Then I changed to another room... The shower head kept dripping, and the staff came later to shake the water out... The TV was very old and not big, and it couldn't cast the screen, but the picture quality was also sparse and there was no 1080p resolution, like the ones from 20 years ago... Then there were very few sockets and it was difficult to plug them in... Later I asked for a power *****, but they said there was none. The next day I couldn't stand it and couldn't plug in the charging socket, so I asked for a power ***** again. I stayed for two nights and the air conditioner was too noisy. I called the staff and they said you should just turn off the air conditioner. Really, who would turn on the air conditioner if it wasn't cold in winter? ? ? I told you it was noisy and you told me to turn it off! ! ! It was really perfunctory! The service attitude also depends on who answers! The breakfast variety is a bit limited, and the cakes are hard... I ate it for one day and didn't want to go the next day. I checked out early on the third day... If it is a five-star hotel at this price, I think it is really not cost-effective. Compared with the current hotels, the location, service, and facilities are incomparable. I can only say that the hotel is indeed fully functional and richly decorated, but it is strong on the outside but weak on the inside! This is the worst experience I have had in a five-star hotel! The old five-star hotel can't keep relying on its past reputation like this! I hope you can make improvements in all aspects!
